[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The report indicates a libFuzzer timeout rather than a crash or exception. The [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz target did not complete processing of the input PDF within the allotted time [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
